const containerRect = container.getBoundingClientRect();\n   298→\n   299→      const nodePositions = network.getPositions();\n   300→      const nodeIds = Object.keys(nodePositions);\n   301→\n   302→      if (nodeIds.length === 0) {\n   303→        return;\n   304→      }\n   305→\n   306→      let minX = Infinity,\n   307→        maxX = -Infinity,\n   308→        minY = Infinity,\n   309→        maxY = -Infinity;\n   310→\n   311→      nodeIds.forEach((nodeId) => {\n   312→        const pos = nodePositions[nodeId];\n   313→        minX = Math.min(minX, pos.x);\n   314→        maxX = Math.max(maxX, pos.x);\n   315→        minY = Math.min(minY, pos.y);\n   316→        maxY = Math.max(maxY, pos.y);\n   317→      });\n   318→\n   319→      // Add some padding for node sizes (approximate node width/height)\n   320→      const nodePadding = 100;\n   321→      const graphWidth = (maxX - minX + nodePadding * 2) * scale;\n   322→      const graphHeight = (maxY - minY + nodePadding * 2) * scale;\n   323→\n   324→      // max amount that a graph can be dragged on respective axis\n   325→      const maxDragX = (containerRect.width / 2 + graphWidth * 0.35) / scale;\n   326→      const maxDragY = (containerRect.height / 2 + graphHeight * 0.35) / scale;\n   327→\n   328→      // Clamp position within bounds\n   329→      const constrainedX = Math.max(-maxDragX, Math.min(maxDragX, position.x));\n   330→      const constrainedY = Math.max(-maxDragY, Math.min(maxDragY, position.y));\n   331→\n   332→      if (constrainedX !== position.x || constrainedY !== position.y) {\n   333→        network.moveTo({\n   334→          position: { x: constrainedX, y: constrainedY },\n   335→          scale: scale,\n   336→          animation: false,\n   337→        });\n   338→      }\n   339→    };\n   340→\n   341→    // Apply constraints after drag ends\n   342→    network.on(\"dragEnd\", (params) => {\n   343→      // only if dragging graph not nodes\n   344→      if (params.nodes.length === 0) {\n   345→        constrainView();\n   346→      }\n   347→    });\n   348→\n   349→    network.on(\"zoom\", () => {\n   350→      constrainView();\n   351→    });\n   352→\n   353→    // force redraw on resetting view\n   354→    const handleResize = () => {\n   355→      if (network) {\n   356→        network.redraw();\n   357→        network.fit();\n   358→      }\n   359→    };\n   360→\n   361→    window.addEventListener(\"resize\", handleResize);\n   362→\n   363→    return () => {\n   364→      window.removeEventListener(\"resize\", 370→\n   371→  // Update node labels when observation indices change, without recreating network\n   372→  useEffect(() => {\n   373→    const nodesDataSet = nodesDataSetRef.current;\n   374→    if (!nodesDataSet) return;\n   375→\n   376→    try {\n   377→      const updates: { id: string; label: string }[] = [];\n   378→\n   379→      graphData.nodes.forEach((node) => {\n   380→        const      node.id === LANGGRAPH_END_NODE_NAME;\n   385→\n   386→        if (isSystemNode) return;\n   387→\n   388→        const observations = nodeToObservationsMap[node.id] || [];\n   389→        const currentIndex = currentObservationIndices[node.id] || 0;\n   390→        const counter =\n   391→          observations.length > 1\n   392→            ? ` (${observations.length - currentIndex}/${observations.length})`\n   393→            : \"\";\n   394→\n   395→        const newLabel = `${node.label}${counter}`;\n   396→        updates.push({ id: node.id, label: newLabel });\n   397→      });\n   398→\n   399→      if (updates.length > 0) {\n   400→        nodesDataSet.update(updates);\n   401→      }\n   402→    } catch (error) {\n   403→      console.error(\"Error updating node labels:\", error);\n   404→    }\n   405→  }, [graphData.nodes, nodeToObservationsMap, currentObservationIndices]);\n   406→\n   407→  useEffect(() => {\n   408→    const network = networkRef.current;\n   409→    if (!network) return;\n   410→\n   411→    if (selectedNodeName) {\n   412→      // Validate that the node exists before trying to select it\n   413→      const nodeExists = graphData.nodes.some(\n   414→        (node) => node.id === selectedNodeName,\n   415→      );\n   416→\n   417→      if (nodeExists) {\n   418→        try {\n   419→ ARCHITECTURE OVERVIEW\n\n**Key Path Structure:**\n- Main trace detail page: `/web/src/pages/project/[projectId]/traces/[traceId].tsx` (router)\n- Trace layout components: `/web/src/components/trace2/Trace.tsx` (composition layer)\n- TracePage wrapper: `/web/src/components/trace2/TracePage.tsx` (data fetching)\n\n**Component Hierarchy:**\n```\nTracePage (fetches data, manages top-level state)\n  → Trace (providers + responsive layout)\n    → TraceDataProvider (tree building + nodeMap)\n    → TraceGraphDataProvider (agent graph data)\n    → ViewPreferencesProvider (display preferences)\n    → SelectionProvider (selected node, collapsed state)\n    → SearchProvider (search state)\n    → JsonExpansionProvider (JSON view state)\n    → DesktopTraceContent or MobileTraceContent (platform detection)\n      → TraceLayoutDesktop/Mobile (resizable panels)\n        → TracePanelNavigation (left panel - tree/timeline)\n        → TracePanelDetail (right panel - details)\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. TRACE TIMELINE COMPONENT (GANTT CHART)\n\n**Location:** `/web/src/components/trace2/components/TraceTimeline/`\n\n**Key Files:**\n- `index.tsx` - Main TraceTimeline component (virtualized rows, synchronized scrolling)\n- `TimelineBar.tsx` - Tree → flat array with pre-computed metrics\n- `types.ts` - Timeline-specific types\n\n**Timeline Visualization Technique:**\n\nThe timeline uses a **hybrid horizontal layout**:\n\n1. **Coordinate System:**\n   - X-axis: Time (0 to trace duration in seconds)\n   - Y-axis: Observation hierarchy (depth from tree)\n   - Each observation renders as a horizontal bar positioned by start time\n   - Bar width = duration × (scaleWidth / traceDuration)\n\n2. **CSS Technique (No SVG):**\n   - Pure HTML divs with `marginLeft` for positioning (inline styles)\n   - Bar width via `style={{ width: '${itemWidth}px' }}`\n   - Background color via `bg-muted` Tailwind class\n   - Border for structure: `border-border`\n   - Selection ring: `ring-3 ring-primary-accent` (when selected)\n\n3. **Key Calculation Functions** (`timeline-calculations.ts`):\n```typescript\ncalculateTimelineOffset(nodeStartTime, traceStartTime, totalScaleSpan, scaleWidth)\n  // Returns: (timeFromStart / totalScaleSpan) * scaleWidth\n\ncalculateTimelineWidth(duration, totalScaleSpan, scaleWidth)\n  // Returns: (duration / totalScaleSpan) * scaleWidth\n\ncalculateStepSize(traceDuration, scaleWidth)\n  // Selects from PREDEFINED_STEP_SIZES array to ensure readable markers\n```\n\n4. **Virtualization:**\n   - Uses TanStack `@tanstack/react-virtual` for row virtualization\n   - Only renders visible rows + overscan buffer\n   - `estimateSize: () => 42` (42px per row height)\n   - `overscan: 500` (large buffer for smooth scrolling)\n\n5. **Tree Structure Integration:**\n   - Left side: Tree lines + expand/collapse button\n   - Center: Timeline bar\n   - Indentation: `TREE_INDENTATION = 12px` per depth level\n   - Tree connector lines drawn with CSS (`.bg-border` div)\n\n6. **Feature: First Token Time (Streaming LLMs)**\n```typescript\n// TimelineBar.tsx lines 37-122\nif (firstTokenTimeOffset) {\n  // Split bar: left (waiting) + right (completion)\n  // Left: opacity-60, dashed border\n  // Right: normal style\n  // Labeled with \"First token\" badge\n}\n```\n\n7. **Color Coding (Heatmap):**\n   - Cost heatmap: Red (high) → Green (low) based on `parentTotalCost`\n   - Duration heatmap: Similar logic with `parentTotalDuration`\n   - Uses function `heatMapTextColor()` from helpers.ts\n\n**Scroll Synchronization:**\n```typescript\n// index.tsx lines 111-121\n// Scroll events on timeIndex → update contentRef.scrollLeft\n// Scroll events on content → update timeIndexRef.scrollLeft\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. TRACE TREE / NODE DISPLAY\n\n**Location:** `/web/src/components/trace2/lib/tree-building.ts` + flattening\n\n**Tree Data Structure:**\n\n```typescript\n// types.ts\ntype TreeNode = {\n  id: string;\n  type: \"TRACE\" | ObservationType; // GENERATION, TOOL, AGENT, etc.\n  name: string;\n  startTime: Date;\n  endTime?: Date | null;\n  level?: string; // DEBUG, DEFAULT, WARNING, ERROR\n  children: TreeNode[]; // Recursive children array\n  // Cost aggregation (bottom-up)\n  totalCost?: Decimal; // This node + all descendants\n  // Token usage\n  inputUsage?: number | null;\n  outputUsage?: number | null;\n  totalUsage?: number | null;\n  // Timestamps relative to trace start\n  startTimeSinceTrace: number; // milliseconds\n  startTimeSinceParentStart: number | null;\n  depth: number;\n  childrenDepth: number; // Max depth of subtree\n}\n```\n\n**Tree Building Algorithm** (fully iterative, no recursion):\n\n1. **Input:** Flat array of observations sorted by startTime\n2. **Dependency Graph:** Build parent-child map via `parentObservationId`\n3. **Topological Sort:** Queue-based bottom-up processing (children before parents)\n4. **Cost Aggregation:** Computed during traversal (O(N) time)\n5. **Output:** \n   - `roots`: Array of root observations (no parent)\n   - `nodeMap`: Map<id, TreeNode> for O(1) node lookup\n   - `searchItems`: Flattened list with parent totals for heatmaps\n\n**Key Code Path:**\n```typescript\n// tree-building.ts\nexport function buildTraceUiData(trace, observations) {\n  // 1. prepareObservations() - sort by startTime, validate parent refs\n  // 2. buildDependencyGraph() - map parentObservationId → childrenIds\n  // 3. topologicalSort() - queue-based traversal (bottom-up)\n  // 4. buildTreeNodes() - create TreeNode objects with cost aggregation\n  // 5. flattenToSearchItems() - iterative pre-order traversal\n  return { roots, nodeMap, searchItems }\n}\n```\n\n**Nesting / Indentation Rendering** (TimelineRow.tsx):\n\n```typescript\n// Lines 36-68\n// Ancestor tree lines (depth - 1 levels)\nArray.from({ length: depth - 1 }, (_, i) => (\n  <div key={i} style={{ width: '${TREE_INDENTATION}px' }}>\n    {treeLines[i] && (\n      <div className=\"absolute top-0 bottom-0 left-1.5 w-px bg-border\" />\n    )}\n  </div>\n))\n\n// Current level connector\n// Vertical line up (if not last sibling) + horizontal line to content\n```\n\n**Information Per Node (TimelineBar.tsx):**\n- Type badge: `<ItemBadge type={node.type} isSmall />`\n- Name: `<span className=\"text-primary\">{node.name}</span>`\n- Duration: `formatIntervalSeconds(latency)` (if showDuration)\n- Cost: `usdFormatter(node.totalCost.toNumber())` (if showCostTokens)\n- Comment count: `<CommentCountIcon count={commentCount} />`\n- Scores: `<GroupedScoreBadges scores={scores} maxVisible={3} />`\n\n---\n\n### 4. DETAIL PANEL (RIGHT SIDE)\n\n**Location:** `/web/src/components/trace2/components/`\n\n**Components:**\n\n- `ObservationDetailView/ObservationDetailView.tsx` - Main detail panel when observation selected\n- `TraceDetailView/TraceDetailView.tsx` - When trace root selected\n- `IOPreview/IOPreview.tsx` - Formatted/JSON toggle for input/output\n- `IOPreviewJSON.tsx` - Advanced JSON viewer with full control\n- `IOPreviewPretty.tsx` - Formatted (pretty-printed) view\n\n**Tabs Structure** (ObservationDetailView.tsx):\n\n```typescript\n// Tabs\n<TabsList>\n  <TabsTrigger value=\"preview\">Preview</TabsTrigger>\n  {showLogViewTab && <TabsTrigger value=\"logview\">Log</TabsTrigger>}\n  <TabsTrigger value=\"scores\">Scores</TabsTrigger>\n</TabsList>\n\n// Tab contents\nswitch(tab) {\n  case \"preview\":\n    <IOPreview input={...} output={...} formatMode={jsonMode} />\n  case \"logview\":\n    <TraceLogView {...} /> // v4 beta only\n  case \"scores\":\n    <ScoresTable {...} />\n}\n```\n\n**Formatted vs JSON Toggle** (IOPreview.tsx):\n\n```typescript\n// ViewModeToggle component\ntype ViewMode = \"formatted\" | \"json\" | \"advanced-json\"\n\n// formatMode switch\ncase \"formatted\": <IOPreviewPretty /> // Pretty-printed with syntax highlighting\ncase \"json\": <IOPreviewJSONSimple /> // Basic JSON with expand/collapse\ncase \"advanced-json\": <IOPreviewJSON /> // Full AdvancedJsonViewer with filtering\n```\n\n**Input/Output Display Technique:**\n\n1. **Formatted View** (`IOPreviewPretty.tsx`):\n   - Uses CodeMirror (`@codemirror/lang-json`)\n   - Read-only editor with syntax highlighting\n   - Automatic folding for nested structures\n   - Copy button + download option\n\n2. **JSON View** (`IOPreviewJSON.tsx`):\n   - `<AdvancedJsonViewer />` component (custom built)\n   - Per-field expansion state tracking\n   - Search/filter capability\n   - Inline comments (if enabled)\n\n3. **Simple JSON View** (`IOPreviewJSONSimple.tsx`):\n   - Lightweight alternative\n   - Tree structure with expand/collapse\n   - No search, for small payloads\n\n**Cost/Token Display** (ObservationDetailViewHeader.tsx):\n\n```typescript\n// Displays with tooltips\n<div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n  <span>{usdFormatter(totalCost)}</span>\n  <Tooltip>\n    <TooltipTrigger>ℹ️</TooltipTrigger>\n    <TooltipContent>\n      Input cost: {costDetails.inputCost}\n      Output cost: {costDetails.outputCost}\n    </TooltipContent>\n  </Tooltip>\n</div>\n\n// Token usage similarly\n<HoverCard>\n  <HoverCardTrigger>{totalTokens}</HoverCardTrigger>\n  <HoverCardContent>\n    Input: {inputTokens} | Output: {outputTokens}\n  </HoverCardContent>\n</HoverCard>\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. AGENT GRAPH VISUALIZATION\n\n**Location:** `/web/src/features/trace-graph-view/`\n\n**Library Used:** `vis-network` (^9.1.9) - A network visualization library using canvas + physics simulation\n\n**Components:**\n\n- `TraceGraphView.tsx` - Data transformation + node selection logic\n- `TraceGraphCanvas.tsx` - vis-network wrapper with zoom/pan controls\n- `buildGraphCanvasData.ts` - Converts observations to graph nodes/edges\n- `buildStepData.ts` - LangGraph → generalized step format\n\n**Graph Data Structure:**\n\n```typescript\ntype GraphCanvasData = {\n  nodes: GraphNodeData[];\n  edges: { from: string; to: string }[];\n}\n\ntype GraphNodeData = {\n  id: string;\n  label: string;\n  type: string; // AGENT, TOOL, GENERATION, SPAN, etc.\n}\n```\n\n**Rendering Technique** (TraceGraphCanvas.tsx):\n\n```typescript\n// vis-network Network initialization\nconst network = new Network(\n  containerRef.current,\n  { nodes: nodesDataSet, edges: graphData.edges },\n  options\n)\n\n// Layout configuration (lines 166-230)\noptions = {\n  layout: {\n    hierarchical: {\n      enabled: true,\n      direction: \"UD\", // Up-Down (top to bottom)\n      levelSeparation: 60,\n      nodeSpacing: 175,\n      sortMethod: \"hubsize\",\n    },\n    randomSeed: 1,\n  },\n  physics: {\n    enabled: !disablePhysics, // Disabled for >500 nodes\n    stabilization: { iterations: 500 },\n  },\n  nodes: {\n    shape: \"box\",\n    borderWidth: 2,\n    shadow: true,\n    font: { size: 14 },\n  },\n  edges: {\n    arrows: { to: { enabled: true, scaleFactor: 0.5 } },\n    width: 1.5,\n  },\n}\n```\n\n**Node Styling:**\n\n```typescript\n// getNodeStyle() returns per-type colors\n\"AGENT\" → border: purple-300, bg: gray-100\n\"TOOL\" → border: orange-300, bg: gray-100\n\"GENERATION\" → border: fuchsia-300, bg: gray-100\n\"SPAN\" → border: blue-300, bg: gray-100\n\n// System nodes (__start__, __end__)\n__start__ → green background\n__end__ → red background\n```\n\n**Zoom/Pan Controls** (lines 232-260):\n\n```typescript\nhandleZoomIn() → network.moveTo({ scale: currentScale * 1.2 })\nhandleZoomOut() → network.moveTo({ scale: currentScale / 1.2 })\nhandleReset() → network.fit({ animation: { duration: 300 } })\n```\n\n**Node Selection/Clicking** (lines 278-287):\n\n```typescript\nnetwork.on(\"click\", (params) => {\n  if (params.nodes.length > 0) {\n    onCanvasNodeNameChange(params.nodes[0]); // Single node clicked\n  } else {\n    onCanvasNodeNameChange(null); // Deselect\n    network.unselectAll();\n  }\n});\n```\n\n**Key Feature: Observation Cycling** (TraceGraphView.tsx):\n\nWhen clicking the same node multiple times, cycle through observations for that node:\n```typescript\nif (previousSelectedNode === nodeName && observations.length > 1) {\n  targetIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % observations.length;\n}\n// Updates URL: ?observation=<obsId>\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. DATA MODEL & API\n\n**Trace Data Flow:**\n\n```\nAPI endpoint: /api/traces/byIdWithObservationsAndScores\n  ↓\nReturns: {\n  id, name, projectId, public, bookmarked,\n  input, output, metadata, tags,\n  startTime, endTime, latency,\n  observations: ObservationReturnTypeWithMetadata[],\n  scores: ScoreDomain[],\n  corrections: ScoreDomain[]\n}\n  ↓\nTraceDataContext processes → builds tree, nodeMap\n  ↓\nComponents consume via useTraceData()\n```\n\n**Database Schema References** (Prisma):\n\n- `Trace`: id, name, projectId, input, output, startTime, endTime\n- `Observation`: id, traceId, parentObservationId, type (SPAN/GENERATION/TOOL/AGENT), startTime, endTime, input, output, metadata, level\n- `Score`: id, traceId/observationId, name, value, source\n- `ObservationView`: Materialized view for fast access\n\n**Observation Types:**\n- SPAN - Generic timing boundary\n- GENERATION - LLM call\n- TOOL - Tool execution\n- AGENT - Agent step\n- RETRIEVER - Vector search\n- EMBEDDING - Embedding creation\n- EVENT - Generic event marker\n- CHAIN - Multi-step chain\n- GUARDRAIL - Safety check\n\n**API Key Query:**\n```typescript\n// TracePage.tsx lines 35-52\nconst tracesQuery = api.traces.byIdWithObservationsAndScores.useQuery({\n  traceId,\n  timestamp?, // For versioning\n  projectId,\n}, {\n  enabled: !isBetaEnabled, // Beta flag toggles between old/new data path\n})\n```\n\n---\n\n### 7. KEY LIBRARIES & DEPENDENCIES\n\n**UI Framework:**\n- React 18\n- Next.js (app router for API, pages router for pages)\n\n**State Management:**\n- React Query (`@tanstack/react-query`)\n- React Context (custom: TraceData, Selection, ViewPreferences, Search)\n- Next.js router for URL state\n\n**Visualization:**\n- `vis-network` (^9.1.9) - Graph visualization with physics\n- `@tanstack/react-virtual` (^3.13.12) - Row virtualization\n- `@codemirror/...` - Code editor for JSON preview\n- Tailwind CSS + Radix UI components\n\n**Components:**\n- Radix UI for primitives (Tabs, Tooltip, Dialog, etc.)\n- Lucide React for icons\n- Custom `AdvancedJsonViewer` for JSON display\n\n**Data Handling:**\n- Decimal.js - for cost calculations (financial precision)\n- Prisma - ORM for database access\n- TRPC - Backend type-safe API\n\n---\n\n### 8. WHAT MnM SHOULD COPY VS IMPROVE\n\n**COPY THESE PATTERNS:**\n\n1. **Virtualized Timeline Rendering**\n   - TanStack Virtual for row virtualization\n   - Pre-compute metrics during tree flattening (avoid per-frame calcs)\n   - Synchronized scroll between time axis and content\n\n2. **Iterative Tree Building**\n   - Use iterative algorithms (not recursive) to handle 10k+ depth\n   - Topological sort with queue for bottom-up cost aggregation\n   - Build nodeMap for O(1) lookup\n\n3. **Multi-Provider Architecture**\n   - Separate concerns: TraceData (structure), Selection (UI state), ViewPreferences (display)\n   - Prevents unnecessary re-renders\n\n4. **Heatmap Color Coding**\n   - Store `parentTotalCost/Duration` in search items\n   - Compute once during flattening, use during rendering\n\n5. **Formatted vs Raw Toggle**\n   - IOPreview component pattern is flexible\n   - Support both pretty (CodeMirror) and advanced (custom viewer)\n\n**IMPROVE OR DIFFERENTIATE:**\n\n1. **Prompt-Driven Trace Analysis (MnM's Core)**\n   - Langfuse shows raw spans (every tool call, every LLM request)\n   - MnM: User writes prompt → LLM analyzes traces through that lens\n   - Two users, same trace = different views\n   - Store \"Schema Lenses\" (analysis prompts) per user/agent\n\n2. **Cheaper Enrichment Pipeline**\n   - Langfuse: Full traces stored, no enrichment\n   - MnM: Bronze→Silver→Gold pipeline\n     - Bronze: Capture raw trace events (cheap middleware)\n     - Silver: Filter/aggregate for user's prompt lens (cheaper LLM)\n     - Gold: Full analysis with context (expensive LLM, optional)\n\n3. **Multi-Agent Timeline Coordination**\n   - Langfuse: Single hierarchical tree\n   - MnM: Coordination view for parallel/sub-agent execution\n   - Show interaction points between agents on timeline\n\n4. **Live Trace Streaming**\n   - Langfuse: Full trace at query time\n   - MnM: Stream observations in real-time via WebSocket\n   - Update timeline as observations arrive\n\n5. **Credential Proxy + Isolation**\n   - Langfuse: Direct LLM integration\n   - MnM: Credential proxy layer for agent isolation\n   - Show provenance in trace (which credential was used)\n\n6. **Guided Lens Suggestions**\n   - Langfuse: Manual graph view only\n   - MnM: Auto-suggest analysis prompts based on trace characteristics\n   - \"This trace has errors, want to analyze them?\" → Suggest lens\n\n---\n\n### 9.
